 mahaan kavi harivanshrai bachchan kii kavitaaon ko padhakar hi mahasoos kiya ja saktaa he, yah ab tak kaa sabase bada bhram he
 This is also because an artist made so many beautiful pictures of Bachchan's poetry collection that by seeing them you will start to feel the significance of Bachchan
 bachchan kii kavitaaon ko rekhaon kaa sahaara dene vaale is kalakaar kaa naam haripal tyaagi (haripal Tyagi) tha
 He is also called public artist
 haripal tyaagi ko yaad karne kii hajaaron vajah hai lekin taazaawajah ye he ki 1 may yani buudhvaar ko unhone is duniya ko alavida kah diya
 He was 85 years old and was fighting blood cancer
 tyaagi kaa janm 20 april 1934 ko mahuwa, bijanour main hua tha
 After passing inter, he came to Delhi and here he got fond of painting and writing poems for the first time
 haripal ek akhbaar main bataur cartoonist kaam karte the
 Later he exhibited his paintings in many cities
 prasiddh abhinayta amitabh bachchan ke pita harivanshrai bachchan kii kitabon ke chitra haripal hi banaate the
 During an interview, it was Haripal who revealed that sketches and covers of Bachchan's books were made by him
 haripal ne isse judaa ek vakya bhi saajha kiya tha
 He had told that once he went to meet Bachchan at his Delhi home, Bachchan said that he who did not read his book, how can he draw his pictures
 bachchan ke aisa kehane par haripal ne unhen tokaa or unki kitabon ke bare main vahiin bataane lage
 After that Haripal got the responsibility to make pictures of Bachchan's poems
 haripal main kai hunar the
 He was a poet, writer, painter, storyteller, art critic and satirist
 haalanki unke rahan-sahan main gramin parivesh kii jhalak milti thi kyonki vah hameshaa jameen se judakar rahanaa pasand karte the

 The departure of Haripal is a big loss for the literary world

 If you go to the police station or Kotwali to file a First Information Report (FIR) of a case and the police officer does not register your FIR, you can take legal action against it
 kisi aparaadh kii shikaayat milane par exiaar darj karne se manaa karne vaale police adhikari ko 2 saal tak kii jail ho sakati he
 He can also be fined
 supreme court ke edwocket upendra mishra ke mutabik dand prakriya samhita 1973 kii dhara 154 or 155 ke tahat thana prabharee kii legal duty he ki wo kisi bhi aparaadh kii shikaayat milane ke baad exiaar darj kare
 Also, give the receiver free of charge
 agar police adhikari exiaar darj karne se manaa karata he, to uske khilaaf bhartiya dand samhita yani ipisi kii dhara 166 ke tahat karrwai kii ja sakati he
 He told that under Section 166 such police officer can be punished from 6 months to 2 years
 iske saath hi us par jurmaana bhi lagaaya ja saktaa he
 Apart from this, the aggrieved person also has the option to complain to the Superintendent of Police and Director General of Police
 iske baad bhi agar police shikaayat nahin darj karti he, to aap court ja sakate hai or maanavadhikaar ayog kii madad le sakate hai
 The judicial magistrate has got the power under Section 156 of crpc to order the police to file a complaint in the case
 supreme court de chukaa he adeshsupreme court ke edwocket upendra mishra ne bataaya ki lalita kumari banaam uttar pradesh sarkaar ke maamle main supreme court ne aadesh diya tha ki kisi bhi gambhir aparaadh kii shikaayat milane ke baad police adhikari ko bina kisi deree ke exiaar darj kerani hogi
 In case of serious crime, the police do not even need to conduct an investigation to register an FIR
 iskaa matlab yah hua ki agar police adhikari ko kisi gambhir aparaadh kii shikaayat milti he, to vah tatkaal exiaar darj karne ke liye baadhya he
 What was the case of Lalitha Kumari vs UP Government: In the case of Lalitha Kumari vs UP Government, the Supreme Court ruled in 2013 the case of police not registering FIR
 lalila kumari ek naaballig thi, jisko kidanap kar liya gaya tha
 When Lalita Kumari's father Bhola Kamat reached the police station to register its FIR, the police refused
 iske baad lalita kumari ke pita bholaa kaamat ne bhartiya samvidhan ke anuchhed 32 ke tahat sidhe supreme court kaa darwaja khatkhataya
 This was taken very seriously by the Supreme Court and sent the case to the Constitution Bench
 iske baad supreme court kii 5 sadasyeey samvidhan peeth ne maamle main sunwaayee kii
 Meanwhile, the apex court issued notices to the Chief Secretary, Director General of Police and Police Commissioners of the Government of India, all the states and Union Territories, seeking answers on the manner in which the police filed firs
 iske saath hi sheersh court ne exiaar darj karne ko lekar hoicourt ke faislon or kanoon ke visheshgyon kii raay bhi jaani
 After this, the constitution bench of the Supreme Court ordered that the police officer will have to file an FIR as soon as the complaint of serious crimes is received
 wo isse inkaar nahin kar saktaa he
 If he does, then action should be taken against him
 supreme court ke faisle kii prationline bhi darj kara sakate hai exiarautar pradesh or dilli samet kai rajyon main online exiaar darj karaane kii suvidha bhi uplabdh he

 About Chhattisgarh 
 
 aapako bataa den kichhattisgarhmen kul 90 vidhansabha siten hai

 chhattisgarh main kul 27 jile hai
 a total of 51 seats in the state are reserved for general, 10 seats for SC and 29 seats for ST
 2013 chunaav main kya the nattejey
 
 
 The 2013 assembly election results were announced on 8 December
 inamen bhartiya janata party ne rajya main lagaataar teesri baar congress ko maat dekar sarkaar banaai thi

 jabaki congress sirf 39 siten hi jeet pai thi
